FROM [MenuSalesItems] AS [m]
LEFT JOIN [Categories] AS [c] ON [m].[CategoryId] = [c].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [Attributes] AS [a] ON [m].[AttributeId] = [a].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a0].[Id], [a0].[AppearanceIndex], [a0].[AttributeId], [a0].[RelatedMenuItemId], [m0].[Id] AS [Id0], [m0].[ArabicName], [m0].[AttributeId] AS [AttributeId0], [m0].[AttributePrice], [m0].[BackColor], [m0].[Barcode], [m0].[BranchId], [m0].[CategoryId], [m0].[CreationDate], [m0].[Description], [m0].[EnglishName], [m0].[FifthPrice], [m0].[FourthPrice], [m0].[HasAttribute], [m0].[ImagePath], [m0].[Invisible], [m0].[KitchenTypeId], [m0].[MainCategoryId], [m0].[NormalizedEnglishName], [m0].[Price], [m0].[PrintInBackupReceipt], [m0].[SecondPrice], [m0].[Tax], [m0].[TextColor], [m0].[TextSize], [m0].[ThirdPrice], [m0].[UpdatedDate]
    FROM [AttributeItems] AS [a0]
    INNER JOIN [MenuSalesItems] AS [m0] ON [a0].[RelatedMenuItemId] = [m0].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [a].[Id] = [t].[AttributeId]
WHERE [m].[CategoryId] = @__catId_0
